client certificates\\n- Sets SSL_VERIFY_PEER to request client certificates\\n- Sets SSL_VERIFY_FAIL_IF_NO_PEER_CERT to fail if client cert is missing\\n\\n**X509_verify_cert** (source/common/tls/cert_validator/default_validator.cc:315)\\n- OpenSSL core function that performs X.509 certificate chain validation\\n- Validates certificate signatures, dates, CRLs, and trust chain\\n- Returns 1 for success, 0 for verification failure\\n\\n**customVerifyCallback** (source/common/tls/context_impl.cc:474)\\n- Custom verification callback registered with OpenSSL\\n- Handles both server and client certificate validation\\n- Orchestrates asynchronous and synchronous validation\\n- Checks if certificate validation is pending or already completed\\n\\n**addClientValidationContext** (source/common/tls/cert_validator/default_validator.cc:481)\\n- Sets up CA certificate list for client certificate validation\\n- Extracts CA certificate subject names\\n- Prevents duplicate CA entries\\n- Critical for server-side client certificate validation\\n\\n### Alternative Validator: SPIFFE\\n\\nFile: `source/extensions/transport_sockets/tls/cert_validator/spiffe/spiffe_validator.cc`\\n\\nProvides an alternative certificate validator with SPIFFE-specific logic:\\n- Uses same `X509_verify_cert` approach (line 177)\\n- Implements `addClientValidationContext()` for client certificate setup (line 108)\\n- Adds SPIFFE-specific certificate precheck and SAN matching\\n- Supports multiple trust domains\\n\\n### Error Handling\\n\\nFile: `source/common/tls/utility.cc` line 457\\n- `getX509VerificationErrorInfo()` extracts detailed error information from OpenSSL\\n- Uses `X509_verify_cert_error_string()` to get human-readable error messages\\n- Critical for debugging certificate validation failures\\n\\n### Verification Mode Constants\\n\\nBoth validators use OpenSSL verification mode flags:\\n- `SSL_VERIFY_NONE`: No verification\\n- `SSL_VERIFY_PEER`: Request peer certificate\\n- `SSL_VERIFY_FAIL_IF_NO_PEER_CERT`: Fail if peer certificate is missing\\n\\nThese are set during context initialization in `initializeSslContexts()` method and used throughout the validation pipeline.\\n\\n### Configuration Flow\\n\\n1. **Context Creation**: `context_impl.cc` creates SSL contexts\\n2. **Validator Initialization**: Cert validator factory creates appropriate validator (default or SPIFFE)\\n3. **Callback Registration**: `customVerifyCallback` is registered via `SSL_CTX_set_custom_verify`\\n4. **Handshake**: During TLS handshake, OpenSSL calls `customVerifyCallback`\\n5. **Chain Verification**: Calls `doVerifyCertChain()` which uses `X509_verify_cert`\\n6. **Result**: Returns validation status to OpenSSL\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
